***slecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a> (381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an earlier meaning of “simple, ordinary, inferior, plain”, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smooth, <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sleht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slihtaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slechter.html>slechter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slechtst.html>slechtst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bad</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ordinary</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">simple</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">common</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mean</span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>

***slee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a> (8987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slede.html>slede</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slēde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slido</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slidô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>sleeën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>sleetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sled, sleigh, wheelless vehicle which glides on <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> or ice</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large/prestigious car
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bolide.html>bolide</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slaihwō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)leie-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bluish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">slåen</i>, and perhaps with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сли́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slíva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plum</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>sleeën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>sleetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The spiny shrub sloe, <i>Prunus spinosa</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">sleedoorn</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> Its stony fruit
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">sleepruim</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slenke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naturally-formed trench filled with water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slenk.html>slenken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make diminish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, causative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slinken.html>slinken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to diminish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slepen.html>slepen</a> (5161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slêpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slēpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slaipijaną</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sleuren.html>sleuren</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***slijmbal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slijmbal.html>slijmbal</a> (13441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slijm.html>slijm</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>. First attested in the 19th century as an unidiomatic term.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slijmbal.html>slijmbal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slijmballen.html>slijmballen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slijmbal.html>slijmballetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">slimeball</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sycophant</span>, reprehensible person <span class="defdate">[from 1920s]</span>
<ul><li><b>1929</b> April 13, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strijd.html>Strijd</a> in Zaandam", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Tribune</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 22, no. 164, page 1.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a> (718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slem</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slimp</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slemp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slimb</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slimbaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oblique, crooked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schlimm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a></i>.

***slims.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a> (31581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a></i> or from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twisted, crooked; bad, evil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schlimm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bad, evil; (col.) sick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 17th century, mostly with meanings such as “bad”, “useless”, “inappropriate”, “evil”, or “wild”, or more rarely “sick”. This last meaning “sick” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> apparently more frequent in Southern Kurzeme dialects; in Vidzeme, this meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not attested still in the 18th century. It became more frequent in written Latvian with the works of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gotthard_Friedrich_Stender" class="extiw" title="w:Gotthard Friedrich Stender">G. F. Stenders</a> in the late 18th century, especially his dictionary, in which <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:krank.html>krank</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> as <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv"><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></i>, and in which <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv"><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> no longer <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> as “bad,” “useless”. Stenders also coined the <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimība</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimnieks</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">apslimt</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimēties</i> (but curiously not <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimot</i>, which appeared only in the 19th century).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lv"><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></strong> (<i>definite</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lv">slimais</b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lv">slimāks</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lv">visslimākais</b>, <i>adverb</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lv">slimi</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sick, ill, diseased <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having a disturbance in the normal functioning of the body or one or some of its parts</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></b> bērns</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sick</b> child</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b>slima</b> sievete</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sick</b> woman</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></b> kuņģis</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sick</b> stomach</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b>slimi</b> zobi</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>diseased</b> teeth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv">ārstēt <b>slimās</b> acis</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to treat <b>sick</b>, <b>diseased</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b>slima</b> ābele</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sick</b> apple tree</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></b> zieds</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sick</b> flower</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv">justies <b>slimam</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feel <b>sick</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv">viņš jau vairākas dienas ir <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b>sick</b> for several days</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>partitief <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stellende.html>stellende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a>   <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a>

***slobber.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a> (99760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span>; ultimately a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slabber</i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slob</i>, which derives from Irish.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">slobbers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Liquid material, generally saliva, that dribbles or drools outward and downward from the mouth.
<dl><dd><i>There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> dried <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a></b> on his coat lapel.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Muddy or marshy <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>; mire.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A jellyfish.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">slobbers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">slobbering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">slobbered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To allow saliva or liquid to run from one's mouth; to drool.
<dl><dd><i>All <a href = vnd.unilang:babies.html>babies</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***sloep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sloep.html>sloep</a> (14796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">chaloupe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">chaloppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nutshell, seed husk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">eschalope</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pod, shell, nutshell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably a blend of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">eschale</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">envelope</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">casing, wrap, covering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sloep.html>sloep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sloepen.html>sloepen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sloepje.html>sloepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small boat, with oars and historically often with a mast.
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">rowing boat</span> or small motorboat carried on a ship.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slokop.html>slokop</a> (99755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">opslokken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to swallow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
